<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ITEM 2.02.</font></b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b>RESULTS OF OPERATIONS AND FINANCIAL CONDITION</b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On July&nbsp;23, 2015, STAG Industrial,&nbsp;Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) issued a press release announcing its results of operations for the three and six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 and its financial condition as of June&nbsp;30, 2015.&nbsp; A copy of such press release is furnished as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 to this report.&nbsp; The press release referred to certain supplemental information that is available under the &#147;Presentations&#148; tab in the Investor Relations section of the Company&#146;s website at www.stagindustrial.com.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As previously announced and as further detailed in the press release furnished with this report, the Company will conduct a conference call at 10:00&nbsp;a.m.&nbsp;eastern time on Friday, July&nbsp;24, 2015, to discuss its second quarter results of operations and financial condition.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information in Item&nbsp;2.02 of this report, including the information in the press release attached as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 to this report, is furnished pursuant to Item&nbsp;2.02 of Form&nbsp;8-K and shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for the purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section. Furthermore, the information in Item&nbsp;2.02 of this report, including the information in the press release attached as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 to this report, shall not be deemed to be incorporated by reference in the filings of the registrant under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended.</font></p>

<body link=blue lang="EN-US">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman"><img width="176" height="70" src="g160651mm01i001.jpg"></font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">STAG INDUSTRIAL ANNOUNCES SECOND QUARTER</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2015 RESULTS</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Boston, MA &#151; July&nbsp;23, 2015 - STAG Industrial,&nbsp;Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) (NYSE:STAG), a real estate investment trust focused on the acquisition and operation of single-tenant, industrial properties throughout the United States, today announced its financial and operating results for the second quarter 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;The second quarter marked continued progress on all operational fronts,&#148; said Ben Butcher, Chief Executive Officer of the Company.</font>&#160; &#147;From the apparent, such as strong acquisitions, continued pipeline growth, robust leasing activity, and a very successful inaugural investor day, to the less apparent, such as the continued development of our people, systems, and processes, STAG&#146;s business and its execution are stronger now than at any point in the Company&#146;s history.&#148;</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Second Quarter Highlights:</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Generated Cash NOI of $43.4 million compared to $33.7 million for the second quarter of 2014, an increase of 29.0%. For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, Cash NOI increased 29.3% in the aggregate compared to the same period last year.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Generated Core FFO of $24.7 million compared to $20.3 million for the second quarter of 2014, an increase of 21.7%. This represents $0.36 of Core FFO per diluted share for the second quarter of 2015. For the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, Core FFO increased 23.1% in the aggregate compared to the same period last year.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Acquired 12 industrial buildings consisting of approximately 1.6 million square feet for $83.8 million. In the aggregate, the properties were purchased for an 8.4% capitalization rate. The acquired buildings were 94.0% occupied at closing.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Closed or under price agreement on a total of $381 million of acquisitions year-to-date, representing over 80% of the Company&#146;s $450 million target for 2015.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Achieved quarter-end occupancy on the Company&#146;s portfolio of 95.0%, executing leases for approximately 2.1 million square feet. Achieved an increase in cash and GAAP rent of 2.8% and 8.5%, respectively, for the quarter&#146;s leasing activity.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Experienced 29.2% retention for 468,169 square feet of leases expiring in the quarter, as one tenant moved out in a quarter of extraordinarily low lease expirations. Achieved a retention rate of 68.8% for 3.8 million square feet over the trailing 12 months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015.&#160; Achieved an increase in cash and GAAP rent of 3.9% and 10.0%, respectively, for the quarter&#146;s renewals.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Raised gross proceeds of $61.7 million of equity at a weighted average price of $21.36 per share through the Company&#146;s ATM programs.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>On May&nbsp;4, 2015, received an upgrade from Fitch Ratings on the Company&#146;s investment grade rating to BBB.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>On June&nbsp;3, 2015, held inaugural Investor Day. The event was attended by over 60 industry professionals and included a full day of presentations and property tours. The audio replay of the presentation, with accompanying slides, is available in the Investor Relations section of the Company&#146;s website at www.stagindustrial.com or through the following link: http://ir.stagindustrial.com/corporateprofile.aspx?iid=4263385</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">1<a name="PB_1_070226_6958"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='1',FILE='C:\JMS\105933\15-16065-1\task7500899\16065-1-mm-01.htm',USER='105933',CD='Jul 23 09:50 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>On May&nbsp;4, 2015, increased the monthly common stock dividend by 2.2% to $0.1150 per share.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company will host a conference call tomorrow to discuss the quarter&#146;s results and provide future estimates regarding acquisitions, asset management, capital markets, and corporate activities. Details of the call can be found at the end of this release.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Key Financial Measures</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, Cash NOI was $43.4 million, which represents growth of 29.0% as compared to the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014. Contributions to the growth in Cash NOI include $9.3 million related to acquisition volume and $0.4 million from same store growth over the comparison period. Adjusting Cash NOI to account for the timing of acquisitions, stabilized run rate Cash NOI would have been $44.4 million for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Adjusted EBITDA was $36.5 million for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, which represents growth of 26.1% over the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014. Included in Adjusted EBITDA is General and Administrative expenses which increased 37.7% as compared to the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014 when excluding non-recurring Consultant Services of $2.8 million. This growth is primarily related to the expansion of the Company&#146;s platform as the Company continues to prepare for future growth and a change in the vesting period of non-cash compensation awards.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, Core FFO was $24.7 million, which represents growth of 21.7% as compared to the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2014. On a diluted, per share basis, Core FFO was flat over the same comparison period, primarily driven by the increase in General and Administrative expenses included in Adjusted EBITDA.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net Loss for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 was $5.2 million. Included in Net Loss is Depreciation and Amortization expense of $27.3 million and a Loss on Impairment of $2.6 million related to a vacant, legacy building.&nbsp; The Company entered into a contract to sell this asset prior to June&nbsp;30, 2015. Based on management&#146;s assessment of the various hold and sell scenarios, management determined that its investment in the property was impaired.&nbsp; Accordingly, the property was written down to its estimated fair value resulting in a Loss on Impairment of $2.6 million for the quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Definitions of Cash NOI, Adjusted EBITDA, Core FFO, FFO, and Adjusted FFO, all non-GAAP financial measures, together with reconciliations to Net Income (Loss) in accordance with GAAP, appear at the end of this release. Please also see the Company&#146;s supplemental information package for additional disclosure.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s key financial measures are noted in the chart below:</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">KEY FINANCIAL MEASURES (1)</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Acquisition&nbsp;&amp; Disposition Activity</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company has closed or is under price agreement on a total of $381 million of acquisitions year-to-date. This represents over 80% of the Company&#146;s targeted 2015 acquisitions volume of $450 million.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company acquired 12 industrial buildings consisting of approximately 1.6 million square feet for $83.8 million for an 8.4% capitalization rate. The acquired buildings were 94.0% occupied at closing.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The chart below details the acquisition activity for the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015:</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SECOND QUARTER 2015 ACQUISITIONS</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsequent to quarter-end and through July&nbsp;22, 2015, the Company acquired an additional industrial building consisting of 201,670 square feet for $12 million. These buildings were under contract as of June&nbsp;30, 2015.&#160; As of July&nbsp;22, 2015, the Company had entered into contracts to acquire another 22 industrial buildings for $142 million. The Company also executed non-binding letters of intent (&#147;LOI&#148;) to acquire four additional industrial buildings for $46 million. In the aggregate, the Company has acquired and is in the process of acquiring an additional 27 industrial buildings for $200 million subsequent to quarter-end.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of July&nbsp;22, 2015, the Company&#146;s pipeline of potential acquisitions is $1.8 billion across 166 industrial buildings.&#160; The pipeline is a point in time measure that includes all of the transactions under consideration </font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">by the Company&#146;s acquisitions group that have passed the initial screening process.&#160; The pipeline also includes transactions under contract and transactions with non-binding LOIs.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The purchase and sale agreements for the properties under contract are subject to satisfaction of closing conditions, and the properties under LOI require the negotiation and execution of definitive purchase and sale agreements.&#160; There can be no assurance that any of the properties under contract or LOI will be acquired on the terms anticipated or at all.&#160; In addition, there can be no assurance that the Company will achieve its targeted acquisition level for 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">There were no dispositions during the quarter.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Leasing Activity</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company executed 15 leases consisting of approximately 2.1 million square feet. The chart below details the leases signed:</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">SECOND QUARTER 2015 LEASING ACTIVITY</font></b></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;">
<tr>
<td width="15%" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:15.0%;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:8.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Lease&nbsp;Type</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="2%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>    </td>
<td width="8%" valign="bottom" style="border:none;border-bottom:solid windowtext 1.0pt;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:8.0%;">

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .25in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Rent change for new leases where there were no prior comparable leases, due to extended downtime or materially different lease structures, are excluded (two leases / 176,000 SF)</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company executed 24 leases consisting of approximately 2.6 million square feet, including 552,495 square feet of new leases, 1.5 million square feet of renewal leases, and 610,600 square feet of temporary leases. The chart below details the leasing activity:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Experienced 29.2% retention for 468,169 square feet of leases expiring in the quarter as one tenant moved out in a quarter of extraordinarily low lease expirations. The retention rate for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015 was 55.9% for 1.1 million square feet. Achieved a retention rate of 68.8% for 3.8 million square feet over the trailing 12 months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015. The rental rate on the renewed leases expiring in the second quarter increased 3.9% on a cash basis and 10.0% on a GAAP basis. The chart below details the retention activity:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsequent to quarter-end and through July&nbsp;22, 2015, the Company has executed three leases consisting of 229,891 square feet.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Portfolio Highlights</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s occupancy rate at the end of the second quarter was 95.0% compared to the first quarter occupancy level of 94.4%, representing an increase of 0.6%. The Company&#146;s portfolio, inclusive of acquisitions and dispositions, totaled approximately 50.0 million square feet as of June&nbsp;30, 2015, representing an increase in square footage of 21.3% since June&nbsp;30, 2014.&#160; The chart below details the portfolio characteristics:</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Liquidity, Capital Markets Activity, and Financial Statistics</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On May&nbsp;4, 2015, Fitch Ratings upgraded its investment grade rating to BBB for STAG Industrial,&nbsp;Inc. and its operating partnership STAG Industrial Operating Partnership L.P. In addition, Fitch Ratings upgraded the preferred stock to BB+.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of June&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company had total immediate liquidity of $375 million, comprised of $12 million of cash and $363 million of immediate availability on the Company&#146;s unsecured credit facility and unsecured term loan. This liquidity is sufficient to address the Company&#146;s remaining anticipated 2015 acquisitions.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of June&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company&#146;s enterprise value was approximately $2.3 billion comprised of $1.4 billion of equity market capitalization, $139 million of preferred equity and total debt of $765 million.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As of June&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company had approximately $765 million of debt outstanding with a weighted average remaining term of 7.1 years and a weighted average interest rate of 4.4%. All of the outstanding floating rate debt is fixed through interest rate swaps as of June&nbsp;30, 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The chart below details the Company&#146;s debt capital structure and financial ratios:</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 13.7pt;text-indent:-13.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)&nbsp;Real estate cost basis is equal to the book value of rental property and deferred leasing intangibles, exclusive of the related accumulated depreciation and amortization</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 13.7pt;text-indent:-13.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)&nbsp;See Non-GAAP Financial Measures and Other Definitions section for definition.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 13.7pt;text-indent:-13.7pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)&nbsp;Adjusted EBITDA divided by interest expense less non-cash portion of interest expense</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the three months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company issued 2.9 million shares of common stock under its ATM programs realizing gross proceeds of $61.7 million. The Company has one ATM program with a total of $110 million of additional issuance capacity.&#160; The chart below details the ATM activity:</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2015 ATM ACTIVITY </font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2015, the Company raised $93.7 million of equity consisting of $71.8 million in proceeds raised through the ATM programs and $21.9 million of Common Units in the Operating Partnership (&#147;OP Units&#148;) privately placed in connection with an acquisition. The Company continues to utilize its ATM programs as its primary source of equity capital. The Company expects to continue to rely on the ATM programs in the future as its primary source of equity and will execute discrete follow-on offerings as required and available. The Company also intends to increase its use of </font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">6<a name="PB_6_073948_3020"></a></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">the OP Unit transactional structure to acquire properties as it provides the Company an attractive avenue to efficiently raise equity capital.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Dividends</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On May&nbsp;4, 2015 the Board of Directors declared an increase in the monthly dividend of 2.2% to $0.1150 per share effective July&nbsp;2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsequent to quarter-end, on July&nbsp;21, 2015, the Company&#146;s Board of Directors declared the monthly dividend of $0.1150 per share for the months of October, November, and December. The chart below details the common dividends declared:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Subsequent to quarter-end, on July&nbsp;21, 2015, the Company&#146;s Board of Directors declared the third quarter preferred stock dividends for its 9.0% Series&nbsp;A Cumulative Redeemable Preferred Stock (NYSE: STAG Pr A) (&#147;Series&nbsp;A Preferred&#148;) and its 6.625% Series&nbsp;B Cumulative Redeemable Preferred Stock (NYSE: STAG Pr B) (&#147;Series&nbsp;B Preferred&#148;). The quarterly dividend for the Series&nbsp;A Preferred is $0.5625 per share, which equates to $2.25 per share on an annualized basis, and the quarterly dividend for the Series&nbsp;B Preferred is $0.4140625 per share, which equates to $1.65625 per share on an annualized basis. The record date for the preferred stock dividends is September&nbsp;15, 2015, and the dividends are payable September&nbsp;30, 2015.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s dividend policy is set by the Board of Directors, which considers, among other factors, a combination of (i)&nbsp;REIT distribution requirements and (ii)&nbsp;recurring, distributable, cash income.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Conference Call</font></u></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company will host a conference call tomorrow, at 10:00 a.m.&nbsp;(Eastern Time) to discuss the quarter&#146;s results.&#160; The call can be accessed live over the phone toll-free by dialing (877) 407-4018, or for international callers, (201) 689-8471.&#160; A replay will be available shortly after the call and can be accessed by dialing (877) 870-5176, or for international callers, (858) 384-5517.&#160; The passcode for the replay is 13614055.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<tr>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP Financial Measures and Other Definitions</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Adjusted Earnings before Interest, Taxes, Depreciation, and Amortization (Adjusted EBITDA)</font></u></b>: Adjusted EBITDA represents Net Income (Loss) (computed in accordance with GAAP) before interest, tax, depreciation and amortization, property acquisition costs, gain on sales of rental property, and intangible amortization in rental income.&#160; Adjusted EBITDA is deemed helpful to investors by the Company as a supplemental measure of the operating performance of a real estate company because it is a direct measure of the actual operating results of the Company&#146;s industrial properties. The Company also uses this measure in ratios to compare its performance to that of its industry peers.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Annualized Adjusted EBITDA</font></u></b>: We define Annualized Adjusted EBITDA as Adjusted EBITDA multiplied by four.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Annualized Adjusted Run Rate EBITDA</font></u></b>: We define Annualized Adjusted Run Rate EBITDA as Annualized Adjusted EBITDA plus incremental Adjusted EBITDA on an annualized basis related to acquisitions acquired in each quarter for which a full quarter&#146;s results were not reflected.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Annualized Base Rental Revenue</font></u></b>: We define Annualized Base Rental Revenue as the monthly base cash rent for the applicable property or properties (which is different from rent calculated in accordance with GAAP for purposes of our financial statements), multiplied by 12. If a tenant is in a free rent period the annualized rent is calculated based on the first contractual monthly base rent amount multiplied by 12.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Capitalization Rate</font></u></b>: The estimated weighted average stabilized cash capitalization rate was calculated by dividing the (i)&nbsp;Company&#146;s estimate of year one net cash flow from the applicable property&#146;s operations stabilized for occupancy, which does not include termination income, miscellaneous other income, credit loss, or vacancy loss, by (ii)&nbsp;the acquisition price, as defined by accounting principles generally accepted in the United States of America (&#147;GAAP&#148;). These capitalization rate estimates are subject to risks, uncertainties, and assumptions and are not guarantees of future performance, which may be affected by known and unknown risks, trends, uncertainties, and factors that are beyond our control, including those risk factors contained in our Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2014.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Funds from Operations (FFO), Core FFO, and Adjusted FFO (AFFO):</font></u></b> FFO is calculated in accordance with the standards established by the National Association of Real Estate Investment Trusts (&#147;NAREIT&#148;). FFO represents net income (loss) (computed in accordance with GAAP), excluding gains (or losses) from sales of depreciable operating property, impairment write-downs of depreciable real estate, real estate related depreciation and amortization (excluding amortization of deferred financing costs and fair market value of debt adjustment) and after adjustments for unconsolidated partnerships and joint ventures.&#160; The Company uses FFO as a supplemental performance measure because, in excluding real estate related depreciation and amortization and gains and losses from property dispositions, it provides a performance measure that, when compared year-over-year, captures trends in occupancy rates, rental rates and operating costs.&#160; The Company also believes that, as a widely recognized measure of the performance of REITs, FFO will be used by investors as a basis to compare the Company&#146;s operating performance with that of other REITs<b>.</b> Core FFO and AFFO are presented excluding property acquisition costs, lease termination income, intangible amortization in rental income, consulting services fees and non-recurring other expenses.&#160; AFFO of the Company also excludes non-rental property depreciation and amortization, straight-line rent adjustments, non-cash portion of interest expense, non-cash compensation expense and deducts recurring capital expenditures and lease renewal commissions and tenant improvements.&#160; The Company believes that Core FFO and AFFO are useful supplemental measures regarding the Company&#146;s operating performance as they provide a more meaningful and consistent comparison of the Company&#146;s operating performance and allows investors to more easily compare the Company&#146;s operating results.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">13<a name="PB_13_083516_455"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='13',FILE='C:\JMS\108736\15-16065-1\task7502001\16065-1-mm-03.htm',USER='108736',CD='Jul 23 22:17 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">However, because FFO, Core FFO and AFFO exclude rental property depreciation and amortization and capture neither the changes in the value of the Company&#146;s properties that result from use or market conditions, nor (as applicable) the level of capital expenditures and leasing commissions necessary to maintain the operating performance of the Company&#146;s properties, all of which have real economic effect and could materially impact the Company&#146;s results from operations, the utility of FFO, Core FFO and AFFO as measures of the Company&#146;s performance is limited. Other equity REITs may not calculate FFO in accordance with the NAREIT definition and the Company&#146;s FFO, Core FFO and AFFO may not be comparable to such other REITs.&#160; FFO, Core FFO and AFFO should not be used as a measure of the Company&#146;s liquidity, and are not indicative of funds available for the Company&#146;s cash needs, including its ability to pay dividends.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">GAAP:</font></u></b> U.S. generally accepted accounting principles.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Location Classification:</font></u></b> We define primary markets as the 29 largest industrial metropolitan areas, which each have approximately 200 million or more in net rentable square footage.&#160; We define secondary industrial markets as the markets which each have net rentable square footage ranging from approximately 25 million to approximately 200 million.&#160; We define tertiary markets as markets with less than 25 million square feet of net rentable square footage.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Net operating income (NOI), Cash NOI, and Run Rate Cash NOI</font></u></b>: NOI is defined as Rental Income, including reimbursements, less Property Expenses and Real Estate Taxes, which excludes Depreciation, Amortization, General and Administrative expenses,&nbsp;Interest Expense,&nbsp;Interest Income, Corporate Sub-lease Rental Income, Asset Management Fee Income, Property Acquisition Costs, Offering Costs, Gain on Sales of Rental Property, and Other Expenses.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company defines Cash NOI as NOI less straight-line rent adjustments and less intangible amortization in rental income.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company defines Run Rate Cash NOI as Cash NOI plus Cash NOI adjusted for a full period of acquisitions, less termination income, less Cash NOI from dispositions.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company considers NOI and Cash NOI to be appropriate supplemental performance measures because they reflect the operating performance of the Company&#146;s properties and exclude certain items that are not considered to be controllable in connection with the management of the property.&#160; However, these measures should not be viewed as alternative measures of the Company&#146;s financial performance since they exclude expenses which could materially impact the Company&#146;s results of operations. Further, the Company&#146;s NOI and Cash NOI may not be comparable to that of other real estate companies, as they may use different methodologies for calculating NOI and Cash NOI.</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">14<a name="PB_14_083528_4141"></a></p>
<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade align="left" style="color:#010101;"></div>
</div>
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='14',FILE='C:\JMS\108736\15-16065-1\task7502001\16065-1-mm-03.htm',USER='108736',CD='Jul 23 22:17 2015' -->

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Renewal Lease:</font></u></b> Renewal lease is defined as a lease signed by an existing tenant to extend the term for twelve months or more, including (1)&nbsp;a renewal of the same space as the current lease at lease expiration, (2)&nbsp;a renewal of only a portion of the current space at lease expiration and (3)&nbsp;an early renewal or workout, which ultimately does extend the original term for twelve months or more, but the renewal term commences before the lease expiration of their current lease.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Retention Rate:</font></u></b> Retention rate is a percentage determined by taking renewal lease square footage commencing in the period divided by square feet of leases expiring in the period.&#160; Neither the renewal leases nor leases expiring include Temporary Leases or License Agreements.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Temporary Leases/License Agreements:</font></u></b> Temporary Lease/License Agreement defined as any lease that is signed for an initial term of less than twelve months; this includes short-term new leases and short-term renewal leases.</p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></b></p>
<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">This press release, together with other statements and information publicly disseminated by the Company, contains certain forward-looking statements within the meaning of Section&nbsp;27A of the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, and Section&nbsp;21E of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended.
